GT Equivalence Verification (MatSci14)

GT: -c0*(T - c1) + epsilon**c2*c3*(T - c4)
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to analyze each candidate to determine if it can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.5450*(T - 352.16) + 1.5180*epsilon^0.6262*(T - 352.16)`

Simplifying: `(T - 352.16)*(-0.5450 + 1.5180*epsilon^0.6262)`

This expands to: `-0.5450*T + 191.92 + 1.5180*T*epsilon^0.6262 - 534.58*epsilon^0.6262`

Key structural features of GT:
- Linear in T
- Contains T*epsilon^0.6262 (T times a fractional power of epsilon)
- Contains epsilon^0.6262
- Contains a constant term
- No exponentials, no trigonometric functions, no logarithms

Let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*epsilon**2 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5 + c6*cos(c7*exp(c8*epsilon**c9))`
No T dependence at all. GT depends on T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** `c0*epsilon**2 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3 + c4*cos(c5*exp(c6*epsilon**c7))`
No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon**2 + c2*exp(c3*epsilon) + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*log(T*c7*epsilon + 1) + c8))`
Has T*epsilon (linear in both), but GT needs T*epsilon^0.6262. Also has exp and sin/log terms that can't be zeroed without losing T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + epsilon)) + c3*exp(c4*exp(c5/(c6 + epsilon)))`
No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*cos(c2*log(T*c3 + 1)) + c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(T*c7*epsilon + 1) + c8)`
Has T*epsilon but needs T*epsilon^0.6262. The trig/log terms can't produce the needed structure. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 7:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon + c2 + c3*log(T*c4 + 1)*sin(c5*epsilon + c6) + c7*Max(0, c8 + epsilon)**c9`
Has T*c0 (good for linear T term). Has Max(0, c8+epsilon)^c9 which for epsilon≥0 and c8=0 gives epsilon^c9 (good for epsilon^0.6262). But needs T*epsilon^0.6262 which isn't present. The log(T)*sin() term mixes T and epsilon but not in the right way. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 8:** `c0*exp(c1/(c2 + epsilon)) + c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon**c5 + c6*log(T*c7 + 1)*sin(c8*epsilon + c9)`
Has epsilon^c5 but needs T*epsilon^c5. The log(T)*sin(epsilon) term doesn't give the right structure. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 9:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*epsilon + c3*epsilon + c4 + c5*Max(0, T + c6) + c7*(c8 + Abs(epsilon))**c9`
For T > 0, Max(0, T+c6) = T+c6 (if c6 > -T). So this becomes: T*(c0+c5) + c1*T*epsilon + (c2+c3)*epsilon + (c4+c5*c6) + c7*(c8+epsilon)^c9.
This has: T (linear), T*epsilon, epsilon, constant, epsilon^c9 (with c8=0). But GT needs T*epsilon^0.6262, not T*epsilon. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 10:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 11:** No T dependence (wait, let me check... c7*exp(c8*epsilon)). No T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 12:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + c2*exp(c3/(c4 + epsilon)) + c5 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon**2`
Has T and T*epsilon but needs T*epsilon^0.6262. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 13:** `c0*epsilon**2 + c1*exp(c2*epsilon) + c3 + c4/(Abs(c5*epsilon) + 1)**5 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon**c8*log(T*c9 + 1)`
Has epsilon^c8*log(T*c9+1). GT needs T*epsilon^0.6262. log(T) ≠ T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 14:** Has epsilon*exp(T*c7) and epsilon^2*log(T). Neither gives T*epsilon^0.6262. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 15:** No epsilon^0.6262 type term with T coupling. Uses sin/cos/log. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 16:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon + T**c2*c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*epsilon + c6*epsilon + c7`
This has: T*c0, T*c1*epsilon, T^c2 * c3 * epsilon^c4, (c5+c6)*epsilon, c7.

GT expanded: -0.5450*T + 1.5180*T*epsilon^0.6262 - 534.58*epsilon^0.6262 + 191.92

Setting c2=1: T^1 * c3 * epsilon^c4 = c3*T*epsilon^c4. With c4=0.6262, this gives T*epsilon^0.6262. ✓
T*c0: linear T term ✓
c7: constant ✓
But GT also needs -534.58*epsilon^0.6262 (epsilon^0.6262 without T). The remaining terms are (c5+c6)*epsilon and T*c1*epsilon. Setting c1=0 removes T*epsilon. But (c5+c6)*epsilon gives only epsilon^1, not epsilon^0.6262. **NO MATCH**
